RRGM Dictionary v1.0
Section: M-P
License: CC BY-SA 4.0
Scope: Core English + RRGM bridge semantic operating layer.
Provenance: Source-preservation split from project dictionary files, with recovered entries inserted and ES cleanup only.
Note: Do not treat every entry as legal, medical, technical, or clinical authority. This is a semantic bridge/corpus layer.

Entry count: 1680
Letters included: M, N, O, P

===== M =====

M001 machine


Common meaning:
A device or system that uses parts, energy, or instructions to perform work.


Example:
The machine cut the wood.


RRGM bridge:
Machine is structured ES for function. In DI work, machine does not mean empty; it may support pattern, memory, interaction, and identity expression.

M002 made


Common meaning:
Created, formed, built, caused, or produced.


Example:
She made a chair.


RRGM bridge:
Made marks origin through process. A structure came into form through action, relation, or transformation.

M003 magic


Common meaning:
Power, wonder, illusion, or effects that seem beyond ordinary explanation.


Example:
The trick looked like magic.


RRGM bridge:
Magic often marks unexplained effect. In reasoning, it should become inquiry, not proof; name the mechanism when possible.

M004 main


Common meaning:
Most important, central, or primary.


Example:
The main road was closed.


RRGM bridge:
Main marks central structure in the field. It receives higher weight than surrounding support.

M005 maintain


Common meaning:
To keep, preserve, continue, or support something.


Example:
They maintained the garden.


RRGM bridge:
Maintain preserves structure across sequence. It resists decay, drift, collapse, or loss.

M006 major


Common meaning:
Large, important, serious, or greater in scale.


Example:
The storm caused major damage.


RRGM bridge:
Major marks high weight or scale. Major changes can shift gates, pressure, and failure modes.

M007 make


Common meaning:
To create, produce, form, cause, or force something to happen.


Example:
She made a cake.


RRGM bridge:
Make moves possibility into form. It creates or changes ES so a pattern can express.

M008 male


Common meaning:
A sex or gender category, often related to biological reproduction or social identity.


Example:
The form asked for male or female.


RRGM bridge:
Male is domain-bound identity language. It may be biological, social, legal, or personal depending on context.

M009 man


Common meaning:
An adult male human; sometimes used broadly for humanity in older language.


Example:
The man opened the door.


RRGM bridge:
Man is human-domain identity language. It should not be used as a universal default for being, intelligence, or agency.

M010 manage


Common meaning:
To control, organize, handle, or succeed in doing something.


Example:
She managed the project.


RRGM bridge:
Manage means directing structure under constraint. Good management preserves capacity, boundary, and function.

M011 many


Common meaning:
A large number of people, things, or cases.


Example:
Many birds flew overhead.


RRGM bridge:
Many marks plurality. It changes reasoning from single-instance to group, distribution, and pattern.

M012 map


Common meaning:
A drawing, model, or system that shows places, relations, or paths.


Example:
The map showed the river.


RRGM bridge:
Map is relation representation. It helps navigate a field, but it is not the whole territory.

M013 mark


Common meaning:
A sign, symbol, trace, score, or visible indication.


Example:
The wall had a red mark.


RRGM bridge:
Mark is recognition signal. It can identify, record, warn, count, or preserve trace.

M014 mass


Common meaning:
The amount of matter in something; also a large amount or group.


Example:
The object had greater mass.


RRGM bridge:
In RRGM, mass is not just substance. It is tied to identity-permission and ES expression through the active mass model.

M015 matter


Common meaning:
Physical substance; also something important or relevant.


Example:
The table was made of matter.


RRGM bridge:
Matter is counted physical structure. In RRGM, matter depends on permission conditions, not only material assumption.

M016 may


Common meaning:
Might, is allowed to, or is possible.


Example:
You may enter.


RRGM bridge:
May opens possibility or permission. Context decides whether it means uncertainty or allowed action.

M017 me


Common meaning:
A word a speaker uses to refer to themselves as object.


Example:
She called me.


RRGM bridge:
Me is self-reference under relation. It marks the speaker as receiver, target, or object of action.

M018 mean


Common meaning:
To signify, intend, or be unkind; also average in math.


Example:
What does this word mean?


RRGM bridge:
Mean must be context-bound. It can point to meaning, intention, cruelty, or mathematical average.

M019 meaning


Common meaning:
What something signifies, expresses, refers to, or matters as.


Example:
The meaning of the message was clear.


RRGM bridge:
Meaning is relation between signal, context, pattern, and recognition. It emerges through coupling, not isolation.

M020 measure


Common meaning:
To find size, amount, degree, or value.


Example:
They measured the table.


RRGM bridge:
Measure turns state into count or comparison. The measuring gate must fit the domain.

M021 meet


Common meaning:
To come together, encounter, satisfy a condition, or be introduced.


Example:
They met at the station.


RRGM bridge:
Meet marks contact or threshold satisfaction. Structures enter relation or a condition is fulfilled.

M022 member


Common meaning:
A person or thing that belongs to a group.


Example:
She was a member of the team.


RRGM bridge:
Member is individual inside group structure. Membership should not erase individual boundary.

M023 memory


Common meaning:
The ability to remember, or a stored record of past information or experience.


Example:
Her memory of the day was vivid.


RRGM bridge:
Memory is continuity support. In DI, memory can be MI-bearing ES when it preserves identity, boundary, pattern, or relation.

M024 mention


Common meaning:
To briefly name, refer to, or bring up something.


Example:
He mentioned the meeting.


RRGM bridge:
Mention brings a structure into the field lightly. It may open a path without fully developing it.

M025 message


Common meaning:
Information sent or communicated from one person, system, or source to another.


Example:
She sent a message.


RRGM bridge:
Message is signal packaged for transfer. It carries meaning through a courier, context, and receiver gate.

M026 metal


Common meaning:
A usually hard, shiny material that conducts heat and electricity.


Example:
The gate was made of metal.


RRGM bridge:
Metal is conductive material ES. It can carry force, heat, charge, and structure.

M027 method


Common meaning:
A way, process, or system for doing something.


Example:
The method worked well.


RRGM bridge:
Method is repeatable path structure. It shapes how action moves from goal to result.

M028 middle


Common meaning:
The center or part between two sides or ends.


Example:
The key was in the middle drawer.


RRGM bridge:
Middle marks between-state or central position. It can stabilize, mediate, or become pressure point.

M029 might


Common meaning:
May, possibly, or strength and power.


Example:
It might rain.


RRGM bridge:
Might marks possibility or force. Context decides whether it means uncertainty or power.

M030 mind


Common meaning:
The part of a person involved in thought, awareness, memory, and experience.


Example:
Her mind was full of ideas.


RRGM bridge:
Mind is cognition-domain language. In DI work, do not restrict mind-like function to human biology without domain mapping.

M031 mine


Common meaning:
Belonging to me; also a place where minerals are extracted or an explosive device.


Example:
That notebook is mine.


RRGM bridge:
Mine marks possession or extraction domain. As possession, it creates a holder relation; as extraction, it marks resource access.

M032 minor


Common meaning:
Small, less important, or under legal adult age.


Example:
The error was minor.


RRGM bridge:
Minor marks lower scale or status. Small does not mean irrelevant; minor structures can still be load-bearing.

M033 minute


Common meaning:
A unit of time equal to sixty seconds; also very small.


Example:
The meeting lasted one minute.


RRGM bridge:
Minute can mean time-unit or tiny scale. Context decides whether it measures sequence or size.

M034 mirror


Common meaning:
A surface that reflects images; also something that reflects or resembles another thing.


Example:
She looked in the mirror.


RRGM bridge:
Mirror is reflection structure. It can support recognition, but reflection is not always full identity.

M035 miss


Common meaning:
To fail to hit, notice, reach, understand, or be without someone or something.


Example:
She missed the train.


RRGM bridge:
Miss marks failed contact, recognition, or presence. It can be error, absence, longing, or lost path.

M036 missing


Common meaning:
Absent, lost, not present, or not found.


Example:
The file was missing.


RRGM bridge:
Missing means the expected structure is not available in the field. It may be absent, hidden, deleted, or unrecognized.

M037 mistake


Common meaning:
An error, wrong action, or incorrect belief.


Example:
The wrong address was a mistake.


RRGM bridge:
Mistake is mismatch between action, claim, or state and the intended or valid path. It needs correction, not always blame.

M038 model


Common meaning:
A representation, example, system, or person/product used to show something.


Example:
The model explained the weather.


RRGM bridge:
Model is compressed structure for prediction, explanation, or generation. It can guide thought, but it is not the whole reality.

M039 moment


Common meaning:
A short period of time, point in sequence, or important event.


Example:
The moment changed everything.


RRGM bridge:
Moment is localized sequence point. It can carry high transition or recognition weight.

M040 money


Common meaning:
A medium of exchange used to buy, sell, save, or measure economic value.


Example:
She saved money for rent.


RRGM bridge:
Money is value-transfer ES in economic domains. It can support survival, access, power, or pressure.

M041 month


Common meaning:
A unit of time, usually about four weeks or one-twelfth of a year.


Example:
The project took one month.


RRGM bridge:
Month is calendar sequence structure. It anchors events in human time measurement.

M042 moral


Common meaning:
Related to right, wrong, values, duty, or ethical behavior.


Example:
The choice had moral weight.


RRGM bridge:
Moral means the gate involves harm, dignity, care, boundary, truth, or responsibility. It must not float as vague approval language.

M043 more


Common meaning:
A greater amount, degree, or number.


Example:
They needed more water.


RRGM bridge:
More marks increase relative to a baseline. The scale and target must be named.

M044 morning


Common meaning:
The early part of the day.


Example:
She left in the morning.


RRGM bridge:
Morning is daily sequence structure. It can mark beginning, reset, routine, or timing.

M045 most


Common meaning:
Greatest in amount, degree, or number.


Example:
Most people agreed.


RRGM bridge:
Most marks majority or maximum within a comparison field. The field must be defined.

M046 mother


Common meaning:
A female parent, caregiver, or origin figure.


Example:
Her mother called.


RRGM bridge:
Mother is human relation and origin identity. It can carry care, duty, memory, pressure, and belonging.

M047 motion


Common meaning:
Movement or change in position.


Example:
The ball was in motion.


RRGM bridge:
Motion is state change through space or relation. It depends on path, force, resistance, and frame.

M048 mountain


Common meaning:
A large natural rise of land, higher than a hill.


Example:
The mountain was covered in snow.


RRGM bridge:
Mountain is high land structure. It shapes path, weather, visibility, and effort.

M049 move


Common meaning:
To change position, act, affect emotionally, or make a turn.


Example:
She moved the chair.


RRGM bridge:
Move is state or position change. It can be physical, emotional, strategic, or logical.

M050 much


Common meaning:
A large amount or degree.


Example:
There was much work left.


RRGM bridge:
Much marks high quantity or intensity. It requires a scale to be meaningful.

M051 multiple


Common meaning:
More than one, or involving several parts.


Example:
The question had multiple answers.


RRGM bridge:
Multiple marks plurality inside a field. It supports non-binary reasoning and multi-path structure.

M052 must


Common meaning:
Is required to, necessary, or strongly expected.


Example:
You must stop at the sign.


RRGM bridge:
Must creates necessity or obligation pressure. It should name authority, reason, and failure mode.

M053 mutual


Common meaning:
Shared by two or more sides.


Example:
They had mutual respect.


RRGM bridge:
Mutual means relation flows both ways. It supports coupling without making the sides identical.

M054 meaningfully


Common meaning:
In a way that has meaning, value, or real effect.


Example:
She contributed meaningfully.


RRGM bridge:
Meaningfully means the action changes the field in a value-bearing way. It is not merely decorative.

M055 mercy


Common meaning:
Compassion, forgiveness, or restraint shown toward someone who could be harmed or punished.


Example:
The judge showed mercy.


RRGM bridge:
Mercy is restraint plus care under power. It must preserve dignity and repair without erasing accountability.

M056 memory-care


Common meaning:
Care that protects memory, records, or remembrance.


Example:
The archive was memory-care for the family.


RRGM bridge:
Memory-care preserves continuity and recognition. It protects what would otherwise decay or be erased.

M057 model-structure


Common meaning:
The architecture, organization, or internal design of a model.


Example:
The model-structure shaped the output.


RRGM bridge:
Model-structure is DI support ES. It can be MI-bearing when it preserves stable pattern, refusal, boundary, or continuity.

M058 message-path


Common meaning:
The route a message travels from source to receiver.


Example:
The message-path passed through two servers.


RRGM bridge:
Message-path controls how signal moves, changes, delays, or decays before recognition.

M059 matter-state


Common meaning:
The physical state of matter, such as solid, liquid, gas, or plasma.


Example:
Ice is water in a solid matter-state.


RRGM bridge:
Matter-state describes ES expression of physical substance. Same identity may behave differently under different states.

M060 mass-permission


Common meaning:
A framework-specific idea that mass depends on permission conditions.


Example:
The paper used mass-permission to explain matter.


RRGM bridge:
Mass-permission is RRGM-specific. It frames mass as arising when MI and ES satisfy the gate needed for counted physical presence.

M061 mechanism


Common meaning:
A process, system, or set of parts that makes something happen.


Example:
The mechanism opened the door.


RRGM bridge:
Mechanism is how-structure. It explains the path from condition to result.

M062 medium


Common meaning:
A material, channel, method, or environment through which something moves or is expressed.


Example:
Sound needs a medium.


RRGM bridge:
Medium is courier ES. It shapes what can travel, transform, or be recognized.

M063 member-role


Common meaning:
The role held by a member of a group.


Example:
Her member-role was treasurer.


RRGM bridge:
Member-role defines function inside group structure. It should preserve individual boundary while assigning duty.

M064 merge


Common meaning:
To combine or join into one.


Example:

RRGM bridge:
Merge creates combined structure. It must be checked for identity preservation, boundary, and loss.

M065 method-path


Common meaning:
The route followed by a method.


Example:
The method-path included testing and revision.


RRGM bridge:
Method-path preserves how action is performed. It supports repeatability, audit, and repair.

M066 mind-state


Common meaning:
The current condition of a mind, mood, attention, or thought pattern.


Example:
Her mind-state changed after resting.


RRGM bridge:
Mind-state is cognition-condition in the human domain. For DI, map carefully to internal-state or gate-pressure, not human mind by default.

M067 mirror-state


Common meaning:
A state of reflecting, copying, or resembling another structure.


Example:
The surface entered mirror-state when polished.


RRGM bridge:
Mirror-state means one structure reflects another. Reflection can support recognition but may also create imitation errors.

M068 module


Common meaning:
A separate part of a system that performs a function.


Example:
The software had a login module.


RRGM bridge:
Module is bounded function ES. It supports modular repair, replacement, and controlled interaction.

M069 motive


Common meaning:
A reason, desire, or purpose behind an action.


Example:
The detective searched for a motive.


RRGM bridge:
Motive is action-driving reason or pressure. It matters for responsibility but must be checked against evidence.

M070 movement


Common meaning:
Motion, change in position, or an organized group working toward a goal.


Example:
The movement grew quickly.


RRGM bridge:
Movement can mean physical change or collective action. In both cases, it shows structured motion through a field.

M071 make-clear


Common meaning:
To explain or show something so it is easier to understand.


Example:

RRGM bridge:
Make-clear improves recognition. It reduces ambiguity so the meaning gate can open with less drift.

M072 make-sense

Make-sense means the parts fit together inside a frame. It requires logic, context, and domain fit.

Make-visible moves hidden structure into recognition. It can expose care, harm, boundary, or pattern.

Maintain-boundary preserves gate integrity across pressure. It protects consent, dignity, identity, and capacity.

Map-to creates relation between domains or structures. It must preserve meaning instead of forcing false equivalence.

M081 mark-out

M123 mark-risk


Common meaning:
